<td class="pi-horizontal-group-item pi-data-value pi-font pi-border-color pi-item-spacing" data-source="related"><p><a class="extiw" href="https://stray-kids.fandom.com/wiki/Stray_Kids" title="w:c:stray-kids:Stray Kids">Stray Kids Wiki</a></p></td>

</aside>
<b>Stray Kids</b> (Korean: 스트레이 키즈; Japanese: ストレイキッズ) is an eight-member boy group under <a href="/wiki/JYP_Entertainment" title="JYP Entertainment">JYP Entertainment</a>. They were formed through the competition reality show of the <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stray_Kids_(TV_series)" title="wikipedia:Stray Kids (TV series)">same name</a>. Originally as nine, they debuted on March 25, 2018 with the mini album <i><a href="/wiki/I_Am_Not" title="I Am Not">I Am Not</a></i>.
</p><p>Prior to their debut, they released a mini album, <i><a href="/wiki/Mixtape" title="Mixtape">Mixtape</a></i>, on January 8, 2018.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FStray_Kids%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pre-debut:_Stray_Kids_and_Mixtape">Pre-debut: <i>Stray Kids</i> and <i>Mixtape</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FStray_Kids%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D2&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The sub-unit 3RACHA, composed of Bang Chan, Changbin, and Han, existed prior to Stray Kids. While the nine were still trainees, Bang Chan picked each member of the group himself. They then participated in Mnet's reality show <i><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stray_Kids_(TV_series)" title="wikipedia:Stray Kids (TV series)">Stray Kids</a></i> (named after the group), in which they had various challenges to accomplish together in order to prove to JYP that they deserved to debut as nine, which was their wish. "Part of what sets Stray Kids apart is their heightened emphasis on self-composition<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-:0_2-0"><a href="#cite_note-:0-2"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>2<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>", and the challenges in the show reflected this, like when they had to create their own songs and choreographies. They released a digital single titled "<a href="/wiki/Hellevator" title="Hellevator">Hellevator</a>" during the show on November 7, 2017. Though two members - Lee Know and Felix - were eliminated on the show, they were eventually given a second chance. It was announced in the last episode that the group would debut as nine.
</p><p>Stray Kids released the pre-debut album <i>Mixtape</i> on January 8, 2018. All the songs featured on it were initially created during the reality show.
</p>
<h3><span id="2018:_Debut_with_I_Am_Not.2C_followed_by_mini-albums_I_Am_Who_and_I_Am_You"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2018:_Debut_with_I_Am_Not,_followed_by_mini-albums_I_Am_Who_and_I_Am_You">2018: Debut with <i>I Am Not</i>, followed by mini-albums <i>I Am Who</i> and <i>I Am You</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FStray_Kids%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D3&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Stray Kids debuted on March 25, 2018 with <i>I Am Not</i> and its title track "District 9". The group announced its fandom name, STAY, on August 1.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>3<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> This was a few days before their first comeback on August 6 with the title track "My Pace" and the mini album <i>I Am Who</i>. Finally, they released <i>I Am You </i>on October 22. The three mini albums, the <i>I Am</i> series, were all released in less than a year and are all part of the same narrative cycle revolving around the theme of identity and self-discovery.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-:0_2-1"><a href="#cite_note-:0-2"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>2<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2019:_.27Cl.C3.A9.27_trilogy.2C_Woojin.27s_departure.2C_world_tour.2C_and_.22Mixtape_:_Gone_Days.22"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2019:_'Clé'_trilogy,_Woojin's_departure,_world_tour,_and_&quot;Mixtape_:_Gone_Days&quot;">2019: 'Clé' trilogy, Woojin's departure, world tour, and "Mixtape : Gone Days"</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FStray_Kids%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D4&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><i><a href="/wiki/Cl%C3%A9_1_:_Miroh" title="Clé 1 : Miroh">Clé 1 : Miroh</a></i> was released on the first anniversary of the group's debut, March 25, 2019. "MIROH" is a word Stray Kids created; 'miro' means 'maze' in Korean, and the H at the end of MIROH symbolizes either heaven or hell, meaning there are two possible places it can lead to. The album tackles the subject of surviving in a new world that might be harsh - in Stray Kids' case, this new world is both celebrity and adulthood.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>4<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> It's with the title track of that album, "Miroh", that the group received their first ever music show win, on April 4.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>5<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>They came back on June 19 with <i><a href="/wiki/Cl%C3%A9_2_:_Yellow_Wood" title="Clé 2 : Yellow Wood">Clé 2 : Yellow Wood</a></i>. The "Clé" and "I Am" series were then connected. For example, the city Stray Kids is looking at at the end of the music video for "I Am You" is MIROH, and the roof of <i>Clé 2: Yellow Wood</i> was where the music video "MIROH" has finished.
</p><p>On October 27, it was announced by JYP that <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Woojin_(Stray_Kids)" title="Woojin (Stray Kids)">Woojin</a> had left the group and agency due to personal circumstances. As a result of that, the mini album <i><a href="/wiki/Cl%C3%A9_:_Levanter" title="Clé : Levanter">Clé : Levanter</a></i>, which was scheduled to be released on November 25, was delayed to be released on December 9.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>6<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> The album included the two pre-released tracks "<a href="/wiki/Double_Knot" title="Double Knot">Double Knot</a>" and "<a href="/wiki/Astronaut" title="Astronaut">Astronaut</a>", and also the title track "Levanter".
</p><p>The group kicked off their world tour <a href="/wiki/Stray_Kids_World_Tour_%27District_9_:_Unlock%27" title="Stray Kids World Tour 'District 9 : Unlock'">'District 9 : Unlock'</a> on November 23, with a first show in Seoul.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>7<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>Stray Kids released "<a href="/wiki/Mixtape_:_Gone_Days" title="Mixtape : Gone Days">Mixtape : Gone Days</a>" on December 26. The song is about the conflict between the new generation, who wants to do things their way and be able to gain maturity on their own, and the older generations, who nags and pushes to do things like it was done in the past. The title is also a play on words, as it sounds like the Korean word "ggondae", a term for old, nosy and bossy people.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>8<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2020:_.22Step_Out_of_Cl.C3.A9.22.2C_Japanese_debut.2C_.22Mixtape_:_On_Track.22.2C_Go_Live.2C_In_Life.2C_All_In"></span><span class="mw-headline" id='2020:_"Step_Out_of_Clé",_Japanese_debut,_"Mixtape_:_On_Track",_Go_Live,_In_Life,_All_In'>2020: "Step Out of Clé", Japanese debut, "Mixtape : On Track", <i>Go Live</i>, <i>In Life</i>, <i>All In</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FStray_Kids%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D5&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On January 14, Stray Kids announced their first English release titled "<a href="/wiki/Step_Out_of_Cl%C3%A9" title="Step Out of Clé">Step Out of Clé</a>" would be released on the 24th. It contained English versions of the tracks "Double Knot" and "Levanter".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9"><a href="#cite_note-9"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>9<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Two days later, it was announced the group would be making their Japanese debut on March 18 with the release of the best album <i><a href="/wiki/SKZ2020" title="SKZ2020">SKZ2020</a></i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10"><a href="#cite_note-10"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>10<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On March 6 and 10, the remaining shows of their world tour, including its entire European leg, were postponed or cancelled due to the COVID-19 outbreak.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>11<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>12<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Three days later, a poster for the group's upcoming release was posted on their Twitter account. On March 19, the members' teaser photos were also posted, announcing their new digital single, "<a href="/wiki/Mixtape_:_On_Track" title="Mixtape : On Track">Mixtape : On Track</a>", to be released on the 25th.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>13<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>The digital single "<a href="/wiki/Top_(Stray_Kids)" title="Top (Stray Kids)">Top</a>", consisting of the Korean versions of the opening and ending songs of the anime <i><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tower_of_God" title="wikipedia:Tower of God">Tower of God</a></i>, was released on May 13. The <a href="/wiki/Top_-English_ver.-" title="Top -English ver.-">English version</a> of the single was released on May 20, and the <a href="/wiki/Top_-Japanese_ver.-" title="Top -Japanese ver.-">Japanese version</a> on June 3. On May 26, the first trailer for <i><a href="/wiki/Go_Live_(Stray_Kids)" title="Go Live (Stray Kids)">Go Live</a></i>, the group's first full album, was released. The album was released on June 17 with title track "God's Menu". On August 27, the music video of "God's Menu" became Stray Kids' first music video to reach 100 million views.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>14<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p><i>Go Live'</i>s repackage, <i><a href="/wiki/In_Life" title="In Life">In Life</a></i>, was released on September 14.
</p><p>Stray Kids released their first Japanese mini album, <i><a href="/wiki/All_In_(Stray_Kids)" title="All In (Stray Kids)">All In</a></i>, on November 4. A <a href="/wiki/All_In_(Korean_Ver.)" title="All In (Korean Ver.)">Korean version</a> of the album's title track was released on November 26.
</p><p>The group held an online concert, <i><a href="/wiki/Beyond_LIVE_%E2%80%93_Stray_Kids_%27Unlock_:_Go_Live_In_Life%27" title="Beyond LIVE – Stray Kids 'Unlock : Go Live In Life'">Unlock : Go Live In Life</a></i>, on November 22. During the show, which was two hours long, Stray Kids showcased a variety of powerful performances, accompanied with technological visual effects, for a total of 22 songs.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15"><a href="#cite_note-15"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>15<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2021:_Hyunjin.27s_hiatus.2C_Kingdom.2C_.22Mixtape_:_Oh.22.2C_Noeasy.2C_.22Christmas_EveL.22.2C_SKZ2021"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2021:_Hyunjin's_hiatus,_Kingdom,_&quot;Mixtape_:_Oh&quot;,_Noeasy,_&quot;Christmas_EveL&quot;,_SKZ2021">2021: Hyunjin's hiatus, <i>Kingdom</i>, "Mixtape : Oh", <i>Noeasy</i>, "Christmas EveL", <i>SKZ2021</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FStray_Kids%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>JYP announced on February 27 that group member Hyunjin would go on hiatus from all activities and promotions for an undefined amount of time due to school bullying scandals. The group would promote with seven members for the time being.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16"><a href="#cite_note-16"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>16<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>From April 1 to June 3, the group participated in the Mnet reality survival show <i><a href="/wiki/Kingdom:_Legendary_War" title="Kingdom: Legendary War">Kingdom: Legendary War</a></i>, in which they opposed five other groups in a competition of performances. Due to his hiatus, Hyunjin only appeared at the beginning of the show.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17"><a href="#cite_note-17"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>17<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> During the rounds, taking on various challenges, Stray Kids showcased intense performances with impressive vocals, dances and concepts.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>18<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Wolfgang_19-0"><a href="#cite_note-Wolfgang-19"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>19<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> For the last round, each group released and then performed a new original song. Stray Kids' song "<a href="/wiki/Kingdom_%27Final_:_Who_Is_The_King%3F%27" title="Kingdom 'Final : Who Is The King?'">Wolfgang</a>", with the theme of "[w]olves chasing music",<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Wolfgang_19-1"><a href="#cite_note-Wolfgang-19"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>19<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> was named after the famous composer Wolfgang Amadeus Mozart. On the last episode, Stray Kids were announced as the winners of the show. Thanking their fans for the win, they expressed their will to work even harder in the future and to remain humble.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Wolfgang_19-2"><a href="#cite_note-Wolfgang-19"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>19<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20"><a href="#cite_note-20"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>20<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21"><a href="#cite_note-21"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>21<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>Hyunjin's hiatus ended at the same time that "<a href="/wiki/Mixtape_:_Oh" title="Mixtape : Oh">Mixtape : Oh</a>" was released, on June 26, and not long after, it was announced that he would be returning to activities in July.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22"><a href="#cite_note-22"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>22<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On June 29, JYP Entertainment revealed that Stray Kids were working on their next comeback, which would be with all eight members.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23"><a href="#cite_note-23"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>23<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> On July 22, the group released a trailer video for their second studio album, <i><a href="/wiki/Noeasy" title="Noeasy">Noeasy</a></i>, where they confirmed their comeback date to be August 23.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24"><a href="#cite_note-24"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>24<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> On August 17, <i>Noeasy</i> had reached 830,000 pre-orders, more than twice the number of pre-orders their previous album, <i>In Life</i>, had accumulated.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25"><a href="#cite_note-25"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>25<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> The album was released on August 23 as planned. Eight days later, the group recorded more than 1,120,000 albums sales, making them the first JYPE artist to reach the million sales milestone.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26"><a href="#cite_note-26"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>26<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27"><a href="#cite_note-27"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>27<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On October 13, Stray Kids released their second Japanese single, "<a href="/wiki/Scars_/_Sorikun_-Japanese_ver.-" title="Scars / Sorikun -Japanese ver.-">Scars / ソリクン -Japanese ver.-</a>".
</p><p>On November 29, Stray Kids released the special single "<a href="/wiki/Christmas_EveL" title="Christmas EveL">Christmas EveL</a>".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28"><a href="#cite_note-28"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>28<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On December 23, Stray Kids released the best album <i><a href="/wiki/SKZ2021" title="SKZ2021">SKZ2021</a></i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29"><a href="#cite_note-29"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>29<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2022:_Oddinary.2C_world_tour.2C_Circus.2C_.22Mixtape_:_Time_Out.22.2C_Maxident.2C_SKZ-Replay"></span><span class="mw-headline" id='2022:_Oddinary,_world_tour,_Circus,_"Mixtape_:_Time_Out",_Maxident,_SKZ-Replay'>2022: <i>Oddinary</i>, world tour, <i>Circus</i>, "Mixtape : Time Out", <i>Maxident</i>, <i>SKZ-Replay</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FStray_Kids%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On January 7, Stray Kids announced that they would hold a fanmeeting titled 'SKZ's Chocolate Factory' on February 12 and 13.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30"><a href="#cite_note-30"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>30<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> On the second day, they released a trailer for their sixth mini album <i><a href="/wiki/Oddinary" title="Oddinary">Oddinary</a></i>, set to be released on March 18.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31"><a href="#cite_note-31"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>31<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> The album topped the Billboard 200 album chart, sold more than 850,000 copies in its first week and exceeded 1.3 million stock pre-orders.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32"><a href="#cite_note-32"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>32<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33"><a href="#cite_note-33"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>33<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34"><a href="#cite_note-34"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>34<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> It also earned the group two music show wins.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35"><a href="#cite_note-35"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>35<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> <i>Oddinary</i> contains tracks exploring a variety of music styles from '90s hip-hop to dubstep to ballads, with themes as different as charm or vulnerability. The title track invites its listener to embrace what makes them different and suggests that being odd is actually ordinary, something that is also implied in the album's name, a portmanteau of the words "odd" and "ordinary".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-36"><a href="#cite_note-36"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>36<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>Stray Kids embarked on their world tour <a href="/wiki/Stray_Kids_2nd_World_Tour_%22Maniac%22" title='Stray Kids 2nd World Tour "Maniac"'>'Maniac'</a> the next month, kicking it off with a show in Seoul on April 29.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37"><a href="#cite_note-37"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>37<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>They released their second Japanese mini album <i><a href="/wiki/Circus_(Stray_Kids)" title="Circus (Stray Kids)">Circus</a></i> on June 22.
</p><p>On August 1, they released their eighth digital single, "<a href="/wiki/Mixtape_:_Time_Out" title="Mixtape : Time Out">Mixtape : Time Out</a>".
</p><p>On September 6, they released a trailer for their seventh mini album <i><a href="/wiki/Maxident" title="Maxident">Maxident</a></i>, set to be released on October 7.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-38"><a href="#cite_note-38"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>38<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On December 21, they released the best album <i><a href="/wiki/SKZ-Replay" title="SKZ-Replay">SKZ-Replay</a></i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-39"><a href="#cite_note-39"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>39<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2023:_The_Sound.2C_.E2.98.85.E2.98.85.E2.98.85.E2.98.85.E2.98.85_.285-Star.29.2C_Social_Path_.28feat._LiSA.29_.2F_Super_Bowl_-Japanese_ver.-.2C_Rock-Star"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2023:_The_Sound,_★★★★★_(5-Star),_Social_Path_(feat._LiSA)_/_Super_Bowl_-Japanese_ver.-,_Rock-Star">2023: <i>The Sound</i>, <i>★★★★★ (5-Star)</i>, <i>Social Path (feat. LiSA) / Super Bowl -Japanese ver.-</i>, <i>Rock-Star</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FStray_Kids%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On December 22, 2022, Stray Kids announced that their first Japanese full-length album, <i><a href="/wiki/The_Sound" title="The Sound">The Sound</a></i>, will be released on February 22, 2023.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-40"><a href="#cite_note-40"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>40<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>In a video teaser released on January 1, 2023, Stray Kids revealed that they would be making, throughout the year, two albums, a fan meeting, a collaboration, a special concert, the music drama <i>SKZFLIX</i>, a 2023 season song, and more.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41"><a href="#cite_note-41"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>41<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On March 6, several news outlets reported that the group is preparing for an April comeback. JYP Entertainment responded that the group completed filming their new music video, although the comeback date has not been confirmed as of yet.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42"><a href="#cite_note-42"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>42<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> On April 24, JYP Entertainment confirmed that Stray Kids will be making a comeback in early June.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43"><a href="#cite_note-43"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>43<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On April 27, they released a trailer for their third full-length album <i><a href="/wiki/5-Star" title="5-Star">★★★★★ (5-Star)</a></i>, which was released on June 2.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-44"><a href="#cite_note-44"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>44<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On June 26, they announced that their first Japanese EP, <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Social_Path_(feat._LiSA)_/_Super_Bowl_-Japanese_ver.-" title="Social Path (feat. LiSA) / Super Bowl -Japanese ver.-">Social Path (feat. LiSA) / Super Bowl -Japanese ver.-</a></i>, will be released on September 6.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-45"><a href="#cite_note-45"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>45<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-46"><a href="#cite_note-46"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>46<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On August 2, all of the members, except Lee Know and Han, opened personal Instagram accounts.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-47"><a href="#cite_note-47"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>47<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On September 19, it was reported that Stray Kids will be having a comeback in November. A source from JYP Entertainment confirmed that the group is preparing for a comeback although no date has been decided as of yet.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-48"><a href="#cite_note-48"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>48<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> On October 5, the group released a prologue trailer for their eighth mini album <i><a href="/wiki/Rock-Star" title="Rock-Star">Rock-Star</a></i>, set for release on November 10.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-49"><a href="#cite_note-49"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>49<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2024:_.22Lose_My_Breath.22.2C_Ate.2C_.22Slash.22.2C_contract_renewal.2C_Giant.2C_Hop"></span><span class="mw-headline" id='2024:_"Lose_My_Breath",_Ate,_"Slash",_contract_renewal,_Giant,_Hop'>2024: "Lose My Breath", <i>Ate</i>, "Slash", contract renewal, <i>Giant</i>, <i>Hop</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FStray_Kids%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On January 1, 2024, Stray Kids announced that they will be releasing one album and one special album, as well as their third world tour, fourth fanmeeting, and additional video content.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-50"><a href="#cite_note-50"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>50<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On April 17, the group announced that they will be releasing a digital single "<a href="/wiki/Lose_My_Breath" title="Lose My Breath">Lose My Breath</a>" featuring <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/en:Charlie_Puth" title="wikipedia:en:Charlie Puth">Charlie Puth</a> on May 10.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-51"><a href="#cite_note-51"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>51<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On May 9, it was reported that Stray Kids will be having their comeback on July 19.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-52"><a href="#cite_note-52"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>52<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> The report was confirmed on June 19 when the group unveiled a trailer for their ninth mini album <i><a href="/wiki/Ate" title="Ate">Ate</a></i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-53"><a href="#cite_note-53"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>53<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On July 17, <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/en:Marvel_Studios" title="wikipedia:en:Marvel Studios">Marvel Studios</a> revealed that Stray Kids will be releasing "<a href="/wiki/Slash" title="Slash">Slash</a>" as part of the soundtrack for <i><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/en:Deadpool_%26_Wolverine" title="wikipedia:en:Deadpool &amp; Wolverine">Deadpool &amp; Wolverine</a></i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-54"><a href="#cite_note-54"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>54<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On July 18, JYP Entertainment announced that all eight members had renewed their contracts with the company before it was expected to conclude in early 2025.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-55"><a href="#cite_note-55"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>55<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On September 13, it was announced that Stray Kids will be featuring on the soundtrack for the League of Legends-based animated series <i><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/en:Arcane_(TV_series)" title="wikipedia:en:Arcane (TV series)">Arcane Season 2</a></i>. The song will be titled "<a href="/wiki/Come_Play" title="Come Play">Come Play</a>" and made in collaboration with Puerto Rican rapper <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/en:Young_Miko" title="wikipedia:en:Young Miko">Young Miko</a> and American guitarist <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/en:Tom_Morello" title="wikipedia:en:Tom Morello">Tom Morello</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-56"><a href="#cite_note-56"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>56<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> It eventually came out on October 17.
</p><p>On September 30, Stray Kids announced that their second Japanese full-length album, <i><a href="/wiki/Giant" title="Giant">Giant</a></i>, will be released on November 13.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-57"><a href="#cite_note-57"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>57<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On November 15, Stray Kids unveiled a logo splash for <i><a href="/wiki/Hop" title="Hop">Hop</a></i>, scheduled to be released on December 13.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-58"><a href="#cite_note-58"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>58<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2025:_.22Mixtape_:_Dominate.22.2C_upcoming_releases"></span><span class="mw-headline" id='2025:_"Mixtape_:_Dominate",_upcoming_releases'>2025: "Mixtape : Dominate", upcoming releases</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FStray_Kids%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On January 6, 2025, Stray Kids revealed that they will be releasing two albums, as well as holding an encore concert in Korea, their fifth fan meeting, new signature content and a SKZOO collaboration.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-59"><a href="#cite_note-59"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>59<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On March 10, Stray Kids announced the digital single "<a href="/wiki/Mixtape_:_Dominate" title="Mixtape : Dominate">Mixtape : Dominate</a>", scheduled for March 21.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-60"><a href="#cite_note-60"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>60<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Members">Members</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FStray_Kids%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="fandom-table wikitable" style="text-align:center; font-size:small; width:100%">
<tbody><tr>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-action="edit-section" data-testid="log-in-edit-section" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fkpop.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FStray_Kids%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D56&amp;uselang=en" title="Sign in to edit"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Stray Kids' logo is written in Bang Chan's handwriting.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-:1_78-0"><a href="#cite_note-:1-78"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>78<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>Stray Kids are highly involved in the creation of their songs. The lyrics and melodies are theirs and, according to Bang Chan, they are given a lot of freedom.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-:0_2-2"><a href="#cite_note-:0-2"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>2<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> They are able to genuinely express themselves and to send the message they want, which is important to them. The struggles and thoughts explored in their songs often mirror those of their fans.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-:1_78-1"><a href="#cite_note-:1-78"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>78<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup></li></ul>
